The user's core requests for this session were:
- **P0: Revert & Redo Mobile UI:** The user first requested a full revert of a previous attempt to optimize the mobile signing page (). After the revert, the user provided new, specific instructions to make the mobile UI more compact, which the agent successfully implemented.
- **P0: New Feature - Custom Tariffs:** The user requested a major new feature to introduce two new tariff types:
    - **Individual Contract:** A one-time purchase for an admin to create a custom contract template for a specific user. The price was set to 6,990 KZT.
    - **Individual Number of Contracts:** A flexible subscription where users can buy a custom number of contracts (minimum 20), with a small discount for purchases over 50.
    - This involved creating backend logic for pricing, payments, a new admin-managed request system for individual contracts, and significant frontend changes on the landing page, user profile, and admin panel.
- **P0: Fix VPS Issues:** The user reported two issues on their production VPS:
    - The Telegram bot was crashing due to multiple instances running.
    - The server disk was nearly full.
- **P1: UI Update on Verification Page:** The user requested to add a language switcher (RU/EN/KK) and a new logo to the public signature verification page ().

Russian. The next agent MUST respond in Russian.

**what currently exists?**
The application is a full-stack contract signing platform with a React frontend, FastAPI backend, and MongoDB. The key functionalities include user authentication, template creation, and contract signing from both templates and uploaded PDFs.

Recent additions include:
- A new Custom Tariffs feature, allowing users to purchase bespoke contract templates or custom-sized contract packages.
- An admin panel section for managing these custom template requests.
- A redesigned user profile page that consolidates all available tariffs (standard and custom) into a single view with a price calculator.
- A newly optimized mobile view for the multi-step contract signing page () to reduce scrolling.
